# User

## Properties

Display Name: User

Description: Person with access to the Microsoft CRM system and who owns objects in the Microsoft CRM database.

Latest Version: 0.8.1

Entity Definition on GitHub: [https://github.com/Microsoft/CDM/tree/master/schemaDocuments/core/applicationCommon/foundationCommon/crmCommon/service/User.cdm.json](https://github.com/Microsoft/CDM/tree/master/schemaDocuments/core/applicationCommon/foundationCommon/crmCommon/service/User.cdm.json)

##### does.referenceEntity

turns all attributes from an entity into one key valued attribute

<table><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Value</th><th>Data Type</th><th>Explanation</th></tr><tr><td>addedAttribute</td><td>{
  "relationship": "hasA",
  "dataType": "entityI...(see Definition below)</td><td>attribute</td><td>an attribute definition should be passed for this argument. the attribute will be added to the entity instead of the default one.</td></tr></table>

Definition:

```
{
  "relationship": "hasA",
  "dataType": "entityId",
  "name": "positionId",
  "appliedTraits": [
    {
      "traitReference": "is.CDS.lookup",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "name": "style",
          "value": "single"
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.requiredAtLevel",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "name": "level",
          "value": "none"
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.localized.displayedAs",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "entityReference": {
            "entityShape": "localizedTable",
            "constantValues": [
              [
                "en",
                "Position"
              ]
            ]
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.localized.describedAs",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "entityReference": {
            "entityShape": "localizedTable",
            "constantValues": [
              [
                "en",
                "User's position in hierarchical security model."
              ]
            ]
          }
        }
      ]
    }
  ],
  "displayName": "Position",
  "description": "User's position in hierarchical security model.",
  "isNullable": true,
  "sourceName": "positionid",
  "sourceOrdering": 170
}
```

##### does.referenceEntity

turns all attributes from an entity into one key valued attribute

  "relationship": "hasA",
  "dataType": "entityI...(see Definition below)</td><td>attribute</td><td>an attribute definition should be passed for this argument. the attribute will be added to the entity instead of the default one.</td></tr></table>

```
{
  "relationship": "hasA",
  "dataType": "entityId",
  "name": "territoryId",
  "appliedTraits": [
    {
      "traitReference": "is.CDS.lookup",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "name": "style",
          "value": "single"
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.requiredAtLevel",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "name": "level",
          "value": "none"
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.localized.displayedAs",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "entityReference": {
            "entityShape": "localizedTable",
            "constantValues": [
              [
                "en",
                "Territory"
              ]
            ]
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "traitReference": "is.localized.describedAs",
      "arguments": [
        {
          "entityReference": {
            "entityShape": "localizedTable",
            "constantValues": [
              [
                "en",
                "Unique identifier of the territory to which the user is assigned."
              ]
            ]
          }
        }
      ]
    }
  ],
  "displayName": "Territory",
  "description": "Unique identifier of the territory to which the user is assigned.",
  "isNullable": true,
  "sourceName": "territoryid",
  "sourceOrdering": 10000
}
```
